tumblr</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">粘合图是查看对象是否可定向的简单方法。</strong>我们可以想象在粘合图上行走与在“吃豆人”中的原理类似，当吃豆人到达世界的一侧时，它可以从另一侧出来。如果我们想象吃豆人在粘合图上移动，当它进入一侧时，它将从同一颜色的另一侧冒出来，而箭头确定了它前进的方向。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">假设吃豆人进入圆环粘合图的右侧，那么它将从左侧出现。这就是正常“吃豆人”世界的拓扑工作方式。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.28203125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/QAEJXB03eMCUQAyHMPQBiaoHf21XIm6icK6CwGocBoPOtEu4u13eSLW6nDHVXwkLJibm4hfUMsE9QVwCcWe6Pruzw/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>图10：吃豆人在圆环上行走</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">现在假设吃豆人进入了克莱因瓶粘合图的右侧，然后，吃豆人将在左侧出现，但上下颠倒了：</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.28203125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/QAEJXB03eMCUQAyHMPQBiaoHf21XIm6icKXPoMXZGianvN3Xo0Z7pzmMelwwANxQgwanvpejbYjVyPb0VB1bz6qbQ/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>图11：吃豆人在克莱恩瓶上行走</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>由以上分析可知: </span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">粘合图能使我们轻松考虑对象的某些拓扑属性，如果没有粘合图，这些属性将难以理解和利用。</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><section data-role=\"outer\" label=\"Powered by 135editor.com\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section data-tools=\"135编辑器\" data-id=\"98252\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"margin: 10px auto;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;text-align: center;letter-spacing: 4px;line-height: 1.8;font-size: 18px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(155, 2, 94) 1px 1px, rgb(155, 2, 94) 1px -1px, rgb(155, 2, 94) -1px 1px, rgb(155, 2, 94) -1px -1px, rgb(155, 2, 94) 0px 1.4px, rgb(155, 2, 94) 0px -1.4px, rgb(155, 2, 94) -1.4px 0px, rgb(155, 2, 94) 1.4px 0px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 2px 2px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 3px 3px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 3px 1px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 1px 3px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 1px 1px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 2px 3.4px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 2px 0.6px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 223, 163) 3.4px 2px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong data-brushtype=\"text\" hm_fix=\"350:283\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">拓扑为什么有用？</strong></p></section></section></section><section data-role=\"paragraph\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>实际上，拓扑在统计领域中非常有用。<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">统计学中一个新兴的研究领域是拓扑数据分析。</strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">有用的数据通常具有某种结构，这些结构具有某种规律或趋势，而数据分析本质上是揭示此结构的过程</strong>。在数据中寻找结构通常取决于我们如何看待数据，即：</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">使用什么统计检验，将哪些变量与其他变量进行比较以及使用哪些可视化表示。</strong></span></p></section></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">从拓扑结构中，我们知道看起来完全不同的事物实际上可以具有相同的结构。</strong>这个想法也可以应用于数据，因为即使在处理相同的数据，若看待数据的角度不同，它们看起来也可能完全不同。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在拓扑数据分析中，数据的结构将会进行拓扑处理。</strong>我们知道，拓扑属性是在不改变其拓扑性质的变换过程中<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">保持不变</strong>的属性。因此，在对数据进行拓扑数据分析时，我们主要寻找在经过各种处理方式之后保持不变的属性，这个过程可以类比于像拉伸橡皮泥一样拉伸数据。通过这种方式，我们可以确定数据的真实结构，并且不再依赖数据的观察方式。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这只是所谓的“现实世界”中许多拓扑应用之一。</strong>其他拓扑应用程序还涉及看起来不同的事物实际上是否是相同的问题，这个问题在处理经由不同的人、不同方式表述的同样的信息中非常重要。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(25, 67, 156);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">具有不同的表示方式的几种情况有：分子结构、地理图、DNA结构和绳结等等。</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">虽然最初可能很难看清，但是拓扑是大多数数学领域的基础。</strong>确切定义拓扑的“使用方式”非常困难，因为它的存在在数学的工作方式中根深蒂固，以至于我们甚至都没有注意到我们正在使用它。直到最近，拓扑学才成为独立于其他数学领域的学科，不断涌现出新</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">的研究成果和应用。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 14px;font-variant-numeric: normal;font-stretch: normal;font-size: 12px;line-height: normal;font-family: Helvetica;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-indent: 0em;font-size: 16px;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb left border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">作者：Luke Cooper</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-indent: 0em;font-size: 16px;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb left border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">翻译：Nuor</span></p></section></section></section></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-indent: rgb(0, 128, 204);font-family: \" microsoft yahei><strong>LIGO-Virgo探测到“不可能存在”的黑洞</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb right border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"385\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"562\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"374\" data-ratio=\"0.5268518518518519\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"width: 578px; height: 304px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MjY4A5YVEocL2hHmx6pqX4Kxpl8OcDBzGp4nUmJujAnLuVWbUpic7ANJ2EKuPpX7O5PqsvGgWUGZfpxF1fnDscA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: right;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(153, 153, 153);font-size: 14px;letter-spacing: 1px;\">图片来源：N. Fischer, H. Pfeiffer, A. Buonanno (Max Planck Institute for Gravitational Physics), Simulating eXtreme Spacetimes Collaboration</span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb right border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据昨日发表于《物理评论快报》和《天体物理学杂志快报》的一系列论文，LIGO和Virgo引力波探测器探测到一个142倍太阳质量的黑洞，这个黑洞由两个质量分别85倍和65倍于太阳的黑洞合并形成。这个合并而成的黑洞，是科学家通过引力波观测到的最大质量黑洞，也是首次观测到中等质量黑洞（100~1000倍太阳质量）。此外，其中85倍太阳质量的黑洞，也挑战了现有的天文学认知。此前天文学家认为，通过恒星坍缩不可能形成这一质量的黑洞。这项研究将帮助我们更好地理解黑洞演化。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb right border-box break-word><span style=\"font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif justify></span><br></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"347\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"562\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"338\" data-ratio=\"0.8472222222222222\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"width: 562px; height: 476px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/MjY4A5YVEocL2hHmx6pqX4Kxpl8OcDBzUCyAVtER4zA7hmrIXd5knWdbCibKScUyUE955NSTcvRcDz12z6ch2lA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: right;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(153, 153, 153);font-size: 14px;letter-spacing: 1px;\">图片来源：Nature</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb right border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在重力的作用下，容器中的液体通常会落至容器底部。但一项发表于</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nature.com/articles/s41586-020-2643-8\" textvalue=\"《自然》\" tab=\"outerlink\" data-linktype=\"2\">《自然》</a></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">的研究发现，在特定情况下，垂直振动液体可以使其浮于某低密层（如空气层）之上，浮力在悬浮液体的下层会发生反转，出现了明显的反重力效应。研究人员向容器内注入液体（如硅油或甘油），接着垂直振动容器，将空气注入容器底部，直到液体开始悬浮。像模型船这样的物体便可在悬浮液体的下表面反向漂浮。此外，液体下部的空气气泡会下沉而不是上升。这些观察结果违反了阿基米德原理，挑战了此前对于液体-空气界面的直觉理解，或有助于进一步研究液体边界行为。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: !important;\">最大规模新冠病毒抗体免疫结果发布：抗体水平在感染4个月内持平</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">近期，在一项发表于</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nejm.org/doi/full/10.1056/NEJMoa2026116\" textvalue=\"《新英格兰医学杂志》\" tab=\"outerlink\" data-linktype=\"2\">《新英格兰医学杂志》</a></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">的文章中，研究人员采用定量聚合酶链反应（PCR）和抗体检测方法，对随机抽样的约30000名冰岛人（占该国总人口的15%）进行了新冠病感染情况检测，并监测了在4个月期间，他们产生的各种同种型抗体水平和持久性。结果显示，冰岛的新冠病毒感染致死风险为0.3%，患者的抗体水平在确诊感染后4个月期间维持稳定，这提示SARS-CoV-2体液免疫具有稳定性。此外，老年人和住院患者的抗体水平较高，而吸烟者和病情较轻女性的抗体水平较低。研究后续将通过更长时间的纵向研究来更准确地计算SARS-CoV-2抗体的半衰期。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 14px;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb right border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"385\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"562\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"374\" data-ratio=\"1.3719879518072289\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"664\" style=\"width: 562px; height: 771px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/MjY4A5YVEocL2hHmx6pqX4Kxpl8OcDBzpra8faPJXLS4j198vFnuqlgxtXVAMXV80qxW5DsGTWcCxre0uRffiaw/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb right border-box break-word><span style=\"color: rgb(153, 153, 153);font-size: 14px;\">图片来源：Sriram Subramaniam, National Cancer Institute, NIH</span></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb right border-box break-word><br></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">最新一项发表于</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nature.com/articles/s41586-020-2698-6\" textvalue=\"《自然》\" tab=\"outerlink\" data-linktype=\"2\">《自然》</a></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">的研究发现，肿瘤中的一些细胞会获得或失去大部分的染色体，这一过程表明肿瘤细胞正在进行演化，筛选偏好的特征。科学家使用一种新算法统计和分析了取自394个肿瘤不同区域的1421个样本，包含了乳腺癌、肺癌等22种肿瘤类型。结果发现，在分析的所有肿瘤类型中，各个肿瘤中不同区域的染色体改变，存在很大差异。一些肿瘤细胞的改变只发生在母系染色体上，而另一些改变只发生在父系染色体上，这些不平衡的变异表明，恶性肿瘤在持续地进行大规模的基因组重塑。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: \" microsoft yahei border-box break-word>·</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: \" microsoft yahei border-box break-word> <strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">遗传学</strong> <strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 5px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 128, 204);font-family: \" microsoft yahei border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">蚂蚁与细菌共生，加深理解复杂生命的演化</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">弓背蚁的细胞内生活一种名为<em>Blochmannia</em>的共生细菌，它能够帮助弓背蚁合成营养，调节工蚁的体型分布；而弓背蚁提供其必要的生存环境。据一项发表于</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.nature.com/articles/s41586-020-2653-6\" textvalue=\"《自然》\" tab=\"outerlink\" data-linktype=\"2\">《自然》</a></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">的研究，科学家发现在弓背蚁的胚胎发育过程中，这种细菌会将前者的生殖系细胞包围起来。对相关基因的分析发现，不同于其他昆虫，包含弓背蚁遗传信息的生殖系基因和调控形体的<em>hox</em>基因均分散于胚胎的四个位置，而非一个位置上。这些基因分工协作，形成了一个坐标系，帮助细菌定位、整合进细胞中。这项研究加深了对单细胞生物与多细胞生物整合，形成复杂生命的理解。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">航空飞行对气候有极其复杂的影响。发表于</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://doi.org/10.1016/j.atmosenv.2020.117834\" textvalue=\"《大气环境》\" tab=\"outerlink\" data-linktype=\"2\">《大气环境》</a></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">的一项研究对飞机造成的全球变暖进行了迄今最全面的分析。研究指出，在2000-2018年间，飞机对人类活动造成的全球变暖影响的贡献保持为3.5％。但考虑到其他增温来源也在迅速增加，飞行对全球变暖的贡献几乎翻了一番，这种快速增长远远超出人们为减少其影响所做的努力。研究者建议，通过利用可再生能源将大气中的二氧化碳转化为合成煤油（不含最能产生烟灰的芳香化学物质），以此来中和飞行中产生的碳，并使飞机凝结尾迹的增温效应减半。 </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 5px;margin-left: 5px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span !important;\">据日媒报道，日本政府正在考虑为所有希望接种新冠疫苗的国民免费提供接种，将优先为高龄人群和医护人员接种，然后推广到所有民众。所有费用将由政府承担，以让尽可能多的人尽早获得免疫能力。报道称，日本的传染病学家和经济学家们，将在政府主导的专门会议上讨论具体接种方案。日本政府正在和美国辉瑞和英国阿斯利康等药企进行协商，计划在2021年东京奥运会召开前为所有国民提供接种。 </span></section><section
